TASK-002 P1 task ✔ TESTS 3/3 #2 PLANNED
Manual Journal Entry UI
Add a manager-facing form to post arbitrary double-entry journal entries directly to the ledger (e.g. mortgage interest, insurance premiums, property tax, management fees). Required to populate the 25 COA accounts that are currently seeded but have zero activity. Prerequisite for Income Statement and Balance Sheet completeness.
  • POST /ledger/entries endpoint accepts { date, legs: [{accountId, debitCents, creditCents, description}] } and writes balanced LedgerEntry rows via postJournalEntries()
  • Legs must balance (sum debitCents === sum creditCents) — 400 if not
  • /manager/finance/ledger has a "New Entry" button that opens a form: date picker, repeating account+debit+credit rows, description, submit
  • On submit the entry appears immediately in the Journal tab
  • Auth: MANAGER or OWNER only
  • npx tsc --noEmit — zero errors

TASK-003 P1 task ✔ TESTS 3/3 #3 DONE
Automatic Monthly Rent Invoice Generation
Generate and issue one rent invoice per active lease per month, posting Dr. Rent Receivables (1100) / Cr. Rental Income (3200) to the ledger. Currently leases carry monthly amounts but nothing creates invoices or ledger entries for rent — accounts 3200/1100 are empty. Prerequisite for the Income Statement revenue side and the collection rate KPI being meaningful.
  • BG job or cron runs on 1st of each month: finds all ACTIVE/SIGNED leases with no rent invoice for the current month
  • Creates Invoice per lease with leaseId set, amount = netRentChf + garageRentChf + otherServiceRentChf, status ISSUED
  • issueInvoiceWorkflow fires postInvoiceIssued → Dr 1100 / Cr 3200
  • Idempotent: re-running for a month that already has invoices does nothing
  • Endpoint GET /leases/:id/rent-invoices returns generated invoices for a lease
  • npx tsc --noEmit — zero errors

Financial Statements — Income Statement, Balance Sheet, Cash Flow
Derive and render the three core financial statements from the ledger. All data already exists in LedgerEntry once TASK-002 through TASK-005 are complete.   • GET /financials/cash-flow?from=&to= returns { operating: [], investing: [], financing: [], netCashCents }

TASK-007 P4 task ✔ TESTS 3/3 #7 PLANNED
Fixed Asset Register + Depreciation
Track property acquisition cost and post annual depreciation (Swiss norm: 1–2% p.a. linear for residential buildings, land not depreciated). Required to show property book value on the Balance Sheet and depreciation expense (4700) on the Income Statement. Without this, the Balance Sheet asset side is significantly understated.
  • Building model gains acquisitionCostCents (Int), acquisitionDate (DateTime), landValueCents (Int) fields via migration
  • Annual cron or manual trigger posts Dr 4700 Depreciation / Cr accumulated depreciation contra-asset at configured rate
  • /admin-inventory/buildings/:id has a "Asset Values" panel to enter acquisition cost, land split, depreciation rate
  • Balance Sheet includes building at net book value (cost − accumulated depreciation)
  • npx tsc --noEmit — zero errors
Read PROJECT_STATE.md, apps/api/src/ARCHITECTURE_LOW_CONTEXT_GUIDE.md, docs/AUDIT.md, and blueprint.js first and obey all guardrails exactly. Preserve existing behavior unless explicitly required for consistency or safety. Before writing code: 1. Inspect the current relevant UI/page/feature entry point and identify exactly where the target section or behavior is rendered. 2. Inspect existing shared components, helpers, workflows, and UI patterns already used in the relevant area. 3. Inspect the backend source of truth for the relevant data and behavior. 4. TASK-008 P4 task ✔ TESTS 3/3 #8 PLANNED
Per-Owner Tax Report (Liegenschaftsunterhalt)
Generate a per-property, per-owner annual summary for Swiss tax purposes: rental income, deductible maintenance (Unterhalt), non-deductible CAPEX, mortgage interest, insurance, management fees, and net rental income. Requires ownership split model on Building (owner + percentage). Output as PDF matching the Swiss Formular Liegenschaftsunterhalt layout.
  • BuildingOwner join table: buildingId, userId, ownershipPct (Decimal)
  • GET /financials/tax-report/:buildingId?year= returns all income/expense line items allocated by ownershipPct
  • Distinguishes deductible Unterhalt (4200) from non-deductible CAPEX — uses existing expenseCategory
  • PDF export matches Formular Liegenschaftsunterhalt structure (rental income, deductions, net result)
  • Accessible at /owner/tax-reports and /manager/buildings/:id/tax-report
  • npx tsc --noEmit — zero errors

■ Auto-detection — features update automatically when you ship code.
  Script reads schema.prisma · workflows/ · services/ · .env files.
  When a signal is found in your codebase, the card auto-marks DONE.

■ Ticket Management (UI) — create, edit, duplicate, and delete tickets directly from the roadmap page.
  1. Start the server: npm run roadmap:serve (starts on port 8111)
  2. Open in browser: http://localhost:8111
  3. Create: Click + NEW TICKET in the Backlog tab or Custom Items tab. Fill in the form, then click SAVE & REFRESH.
  4. Edit: Click ✎ EDIT on any custom item card to open the form pre-filled with that ticket’s data.
  5. Duplicate: Click ⎘ DUP to clone a ticket (status resets to planned, title gets “(copy)” suffix).
  6. Delete: Click ✖ to remove a ticket (with confirmation prompt).
  Every save writes to ROADMAP.json → regenerates roadmap.html → reloads the page.

■ Ticket Management (CLI) — alternative via terminal:
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js create — guided interactive creation
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js edit <ID> — edit a ticket by ID
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js start|complete|block <ID> — change ticket status
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js validate <ID> — guided validation wizard + mark done
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js list — list all custom items
  node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js next — show next recommended item

■ Adding tickets via JSON — edit ROADMAP.json → custom_items[]:
{
  "id": "US-001",       // auto-generated, or US-XXX | TASK-XXX | BUG-XXX | SPK-XXX
  "phase": "P1",       // P0 | P1 | P2 | P3 | P4 | P5
  "title": "As a landlord, I want ...",
  "type": "user_story", // user_story | task | bug | spike
  "order": 1,         // chronological sequence within phase
  "depends_on": ["F-P0-001"],   // references to dependencies
  "parent_feature": "F-P1-001",// attach to a feature
  "acceptance_criteria": ["..."],
  "required_tests": ["..."],
  "test_protocol": "1. npx tsc --noEmit\n2. npm test",
  "validation_checklist": ["..."],
  "post_validation": ["..."],
  "persona": "owner",   // owner | tenant | manager | contractor
  "ticket": "GH-142",  // GitHub / Linear / Jira ref, or null
  "status": "planned",  // planned | in_progress | done | blocked
  "notes": "additional context"
}
■ Regenerating
  node scripts/generate-roadmap.js — generate once
  npm run roadmap:watch — watch mode (auto-regenerates on schema or ROADMAP.json change)
  npm run roadmap:serve — serve with live API on port 8111 (auto-regenerates on ticket save)
  Open http://localhost:8111 or use VS Code Live Server on docs/roadmap.html

■ Wiring a new feature for auto-detection — add a detection block to features[] in ROADMAP.json:
  model_exists · model_field · enum_exists · workflow_exists · file_exists · page_exists · env_key

■ Required fields for new tickets
  title · phase · order · type · acceptance_criteria (1+) · required_tests (1+) · test_protocol · validation_checklist (1+) · post_validation (1+)
  Dependency refs must point to existing feature/slice/custom IDs. Parent feature must exist in ROADMAP.json.

■ Testing metadata gates
  • A ticket cannot be saved without required_tests, test_protocol, and validation_checklist.
  • A ticket cannot be marked in_progress without a test_protocol and required_tests.
  • A ticket cannot be marked done/validated unless validation_checklist exists.

■ Validation Workflow — the preferred way to mark a ticket done:
  1. Click ✓ VALIDATE on any ticket card with complete testing metadata.
  2. Step 1: Confirm each test protocol step was executed (check all boxes).
  3. Step 2: Confirm each validation checklist item is met (check all boxes).
  4. Step 3: Run context refresh (auto-refreshes blueprint + roadmap via server API).
    • Review manual targets: PROJECT_STATE.md · ARCHITECTURE_LOW_CONTEXT_GUIDE.md · docs/AUDIT.md · SCHEMA_REFERENCE.md
  5. Click ✓ MARK VALIDATED → ticket status → done + validated_at timestamp recorded.
  CLI equivalent: node scripts/roadmap-ticket.js validate <ID>
  API equivalent: POST /api/tickets/:id/validate with { protocol_confirmed: true, checklist_confirmed: true }

■ Context Refresh API
  POST /api/context-refresh — runs blueprint + roadmap generation, returns auto + manual targets.

■ Refresh Top 5 — live-refresh the "Next Recommended — Top 5" panel:
  • Click ↻ REFRESH TOP 5 in the rec panel header (requires roadmap server running).
  • The server re-reads ROADMAP.json, re-scans the codebase, and runs the full 9-rule ranking engine.
  • Updated recommendations replace the current cards without a page reload (tabs/filters preserved).
  • Each card shows: movement badge (↑/↓/NEW/—), rank, reasons, and phase.
  • A timestamp shows when the recommendations were last refreshed.
  • API: POST /api/recommendations — returns JSON with ranked items + movement data.
  • File: docs/roadmap-recs.json — written on every generation with full recommendation data.
  • Prioritisation: phase order → unblockers → small scope → testing metadata complete.
